<div id="review_1051492912" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1051492912" />
    <a title="Jamie-leigh Haughn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17182207-jamie-leigh-haughn"><img alt="Jamie-leigh Haughn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483227714p2/17182207.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1051492912?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie-leigh Haughn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie-leigh Haughn" href="/user/show/17182207-jamie-leigh-haughn">Jamie-leigh Haughn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17182207-jamie-leigh-haughn?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1051492912" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11291200894255584670">How cute was this book? Like seriously, so adorable! <br/><br/>Over all I think this book is really a fantastic Holiday read, I'm a huge fan of how it incorporated different Holidays and traditions, not just focusing solely on Christmas. I generally really enjoyed the stories, I found the contemporaries to be more enjoyable than any of the fantastical stories. With each story being only around 30 pages it was difficult to understand and get into any of the concepts that weren't straight contemporary. I ha</span>
  <span id="freeText11291200894255584670" style="display:none">How cute was this book? Like seriously, so adorable! <br /><br />Over all I think this book is really a fantastic Holiday read, I'm a huge fan of how it incorporated different Holidays and traditions, not just focusing solely on Christmas. I generally really enjoyed the stories, I found the contemporaries to be more enjoyable than any of the fantastical stories. With each story being only around 30 pages it was difficult to understand and get into any of the concepts that weren't straight contemporary. I had some I liked more than others and I've rated each story individually.<br /><br />Midnights - Rainbow Rowell : 5/5 - This started off the book with a bang, Rainbow Rowell does it again! I did not want this story to end, it was only 30 pages and I was so invested in the story and loved the characters, this was by far my favourite part of the book!<br /><br />The Lady and the Fox - Kelly Link : 2/5 - This was not a good follow up to the first story, I was really quite disappointed in this one. I found it kind of boring and a bit confusing. there was a magical aspect that was pretty cool, but at the same time it wasn't explained very well and I couldn't connect with the characters at all.<br /><br />Angels in the Snow - Matt De La Pena : 3/5 - This was a pretty cute story, I liked the characters and found an easy connection with Haley. That being said the story was a little slow and not my favourite, but still pretty cute!<br /><br />Polaris is Where You'll Find Me - Jenny Han : 4/5 - Now this was a Christmasy read! Full of elves and love and Christmas magic, I thought this was very enjoyable! Even though it was set in a different type world, it worked and it didn't need much explanation, so adorable! <br /><br />It's a Yuletide Miracle, Charlie Brown - Stephanie Perkins : 5/5 - I loved this story! The characters were too cute and their little romance warmed my heart! I loved North, he was one of my favourite guys from all the stories, such a sweetheart! <br /><br />Your Temporary Santa - David Levithan : 3/5 - This story was pretty meh for me, I felt no connection with the characters. I thought it was a cute concept but nothing was really explained. The two main characters were so separated throughout most of the story that I couldn't feel a connection between them. The story was cute, but I wanted more.<br /><br />Krampuslauf - Holly Black : 3/5 - This was a fun story that started off promising but kind of slacked nearing the end. I thought the traditions were really interesting and I loved reading about them, and even the party planning aspect as neat. However, I wasn't a fan of the magical elements because I just felt like it wasn't explained very well and the characters were kind of annoying. Still, not a bad read.<br /><br />What the Hell Have You Done, Sophie Roth? - Gayle Forman : 5/5 - Oh I loved this story, I loved loved loved it!! The characters were just so adorable and their relationship and interactions were really fun to read! This one left me wanting more and I wish this was a whole book by itself!<br /><br />Beer Buckets and Baby Jesus - Myra McEntire : 3/5 - This was a fun story, I think it wasn't my overall favourite because I'm really not into the "bad boy" type characters. But Vaughn grew on me by the end and I thought this was a nice fast paced save the day type of story.<br /><br />Welcome to Christmas, CA - Kiersten White : 4/5 - I really enjoyed this story! I wish there was a bit more connection between the characters but overall I thought it was super cute and fun to read. I also feel like this would make the cutest Christmas movie! I'd watch that!!<br /><br />Star of Bethlehem - Ally Carter : 5/5 - SO CUTE. I loved this story start to finish. I even found the twist/secret reveal at the end to be really surprising. Another favourite, how cute was Ethan's family? Loved them!<br /><br />The Girl Who Woke the Dreamer - Laini Taylor : 2/5 - This one was another disappointment for me. I think I just need more time and detail to get into stories like this with more magical elements, etc. <br /><br />Overall, I definitely recommend this book for a nice holiday read! I like how the stories don't intertwine so really you can just pick this up and read one or two stories a year if you wanted! LOVED IT!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11291200894255584670" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_816123512" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/816123512" />
    <a title="Stacey (prettybooks)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3533262-stacey-prettybooks"><img alt="Stacey (prettybooks)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577577052p2/3533262.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/816123512?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey (prettybooks)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey (prettybooks)" href="/user/show/3533262-stacey-prettybooks">Stacey (prettybooks)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3533262-stacey-prettybooks?shelf=read-in-my-twenties">read-in-my-twenties</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer816123512" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8686502642428138968">If you had asked me last year what kind of story I wanted to see more of, I'd have said Christmas YA. In my opinion, there just isn't enough, so when I saw Stephanie Perkins' announcement that she would be editing a collection of twelve festive YA stories published this year, I couldn't have been more excited. I pre-ordered a copy and somehow resisted reading straight away. As soon as it turned 1st December, I put up the Christmas tree, bought a festive mug (for festive hot chocolate, obviously)</span>
  <span id="freeText8686502642428138968" style="display:none">If you had asked me last year what kind of story I wanted to see more of, I'd have said Christmas YA. In my opinion, there just isn't enough, so when I saw Stephanie Perkins' announcement that she would be editing a collection of twelve festive YA stories published this year, I couldn't have been more excited. I pre-ordered a copy and somehow resisted reading straight away. As soon as it turned 1st December, I put up the Christmas tree, bought a festive mug (for festive hot chocolate, obviously) and got stuck in to <em>My True Love Gave to Me</em>.<br /><br />I loved the collection as a whole, even if I didn't enjoy every story equally (because that rarely happens with me and short story anthologies), but here's a little bit about a few of my favourites: I am guilty of following the crowd because the stories by <strong>Rainbow Rowell</strong> – about the brewing relationship between two friends over four New Year's Eves – and <strong>Stephanie Perkins</strong>' – about a girl who's building the courage to ask the boy with a beautiful voice for help (buying a Christmas tree from his family in the process!) – were my favourites. I love really cute contemporary Christmas YA the most, so it's unsurprising that I enjoyed these two. I loved that both of these stories were about a girl and a boy (a little quirky and comfortably witty) getting to know each other, from two best friends to two strangers. I'd quite happy read full length versions of both!<br /><br />I hadn't read anything else by <strong>Matt De La Peña</strong> before, but I loved <em>Angels in the Snow</em>, a contemporary story about a cat-sitting student and the girl next door. I even enjoyed the fantasy/magical realism stories, in particular <strong>Holly Black</strong>'s <em>Krampuslauf</em>, although that might be because I was rooting for the main character and a little bit of revenge… It's a brilliantly diverse selection, so you're sure to find one you'll love.<br /><br /><em>My True Love Gave to Me</em> is a completely adorable and wonderfully festive collection of Christmas YA for everyone who loves wintertime romance. I'm sure it will become a book I keep coming back to each year – bring on Christmas 2015!<em>
  <br />
</em></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1813568803" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8230431954058578344">My True Love Gave To Me is a collection of 12 stories covering multiple holidays such as New Year's, Hanukkah, the Winter Solstices and of obviously Christmas. As most books containing multiple stories written by multiple writers this book was a mixed bag. There were some stories I loved like Krampuslauf, Its A Yuletide Miracle, Charlie Brown, Angels In The Snow and the very last story The Girl Who Woke The Dreamer by Laini Taylor. The Girl Who Woke The Dreamer was in my opinion ( and since this</span>
  <span id="freeText8230431954058578344" style="display:none">My True Love Gave To Me is a collection of 12 stories covering multiple holidays such as New Year's, Hanukkah, the Winter Solstices and of obviously Christmas. As most books containing multiple stories written by multiple writers this book was a mixed bag. There were some stories I loved like Krampuslauf, Its A Yuletide Miracle, Charlie Brown, Angels In The Snow and the very last story The Girl Who Woke The Dreamer by Laini Taylor. The Girl Who Woke The Dreamer was in my opinion ( and since this is my review my opinion is the only one that matters) the most romantic of the stories. I didn't want it to end. <br /><br />Now on to the stories I didn't love Polaris Is Where You'll Find Me, everyone else loved this story but it didn't do it for me. Your Temporary Santa was as stated in my update just meh! I read it yesterday but can't remember a word of it. What The Hell Have You Done, Sophie Roth, it was boring and like Your Temporary Santa it was completely forgettable. <br /><br />I would also like to make an amendment, immediately after reading Midnight the first story in the collection authored by Rainbow Rowell I only gave it 3 stars but now I'm upping it to 5 stars. I couldn't get that story out of my head as I read the rest of the collection, so I reread it after finishing the book and realised I was completely in love with that story. <br /><br />Recommended if you love Hallmark Christmas Movies and/or YA novels.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Helene Jeppesen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Helene Jeppesen" href="/user/show/21992464-helene-jeppesen">Helene Jeppesen</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1462279749" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15787160327631921870">At first, I was thrilled with this book. I loved all the cute stories, and I loved how they got me in the mood for Christmas. Especially Matt de la Pena's and Stephanie Perkins' stories put a smile on my face (despite the fact that Perkins' characters didn't act like a 19-year-olds!). Yes, some of the stories were a little bit too unrealistic, or too simple, but I still enjoyed them. <br/>Then came Ally Carter's story and that's when things started falling apart. This story was highly unrealistic in </span>
  <span id="freeText15787160327631921870" style="display:none">At first, I was thrilled with this book. I loved all the cute stories, and I loved how they got me in the mood for Christmas. Especially Matt de la Pena's and Stephanie Perkins' stories put a smile on my face (despite the fact that Perkins' characters didn't act like a 19-year-olds!). Yes, some of the stories were a little bit too unrealistic, or too simple, but I still enjoyed them. <br />Then came Ally Carter's story and that's when things started falling apart. This story was highly unrealistic in my opinion, and it made me realise how all of the other stories are basically about unrealistic insta-love. I stand by my first impression: That they are cute and get you in the mood for Christmas. They all leave an impression on you, whether it's a good, lasting one or a rather bad one. But the thing is that most of these stories are shallow. It seems like Stephanie Perkins asked for everyone to write a romance story with a happy ending, because apparently that's all people want to read for Christmas? I at least missed some more depth to them. <br />Nevertheless, this was definitely CUTE, and my frustrations aside it did get me in the mood for Christmas. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15787160327631921870" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10150016242773662408">MIDNIGHTS - 5 stars<br/>This one was a little confusing at the start starting in 2014 then going back a few years then jumping back to 2014.   <span id="freeText10150016242773662408" style="display:none">MIDNIGHTS - 5 stars<br />This one was a little confusing at the start starting in 2014 then going back a few years then jumping back to 2014. After the confusion I loved it. I really enjoyed seeing the glimpse of the friendship and how it grew over time to something more. Loved this one and would have liked to have seen more.<br /><br />THE LADY AND THE FOX - 2 stars<br />This one is very confusing. Midnights was nothing compared to this one. I can't say I really enjoyed it. Miranda was horrible to Daniel when he went to visit her and what was Fenny? A ghost? Seriously what was with all the rules and what was he. And who was the lady trying to make him go back? I just feel it had left me with too many questions. It is nice they can have a life together though.<br /><br />ANGELS IN THE SNOW - 4 stars<br />I really felt sorry for Shy. First of all because of the name he was given but also because he had to starve until Haley went through the kitchen. I really enjoyed this one though. I liked Haley's confession at the end, it was supper cute after we knew that Shy didn't know a think about plumbing but went up anyway. The game they played before she took a shower in his apartment everything was cute and actually quite fun.<br /><br />POLARIS IS WHERE YOU'LL FIND ME - 5 stars<br />I was really excited about this one as it was written by Jenny Han and I love her! I loved this short story although I think it could have been longer. I lived reading it and it kind of reminded me of the movie 'elf'. I also would have like to see some romance between Lars and Natty after she got his address and if she decided to stay at the North Pole or leave to be with humans.<br /><br />IT'S A YULETIDE MIRACLE, CHARLIE BROWN - 5 stars<br />I was also really excited to read this one as Stephanie Perkins wrote it and it did not disappoint. I wanted more, I didn't want it to end. The line 'You don't realise I'm willing to do anything to stay in your company' made my heart explode. This was such an adorable read and would recommend.<br /><br />YOUR TEMPORARY SANTA - 1 star<br />I actually didn't think much of this one. Connor wanted his boyfriend to dress up like Santa and wake his sister up by shaking her door so she would catch Santa putting the presents under the tree. I guess that was nice of Connor to do that for his little sister so she would still believe but it was a little boring and kinda feels like a book filler.<br /><br />KRAMPUSLAUF - 2 stars<br />I didn't really enjoy this one. It was just a little to weird and some dark things in it to. Well not to dark but I just didn't like it. They only thing I did like was that Hanna had made up a pretend boyfriend and wanted him to be real, she go her wish but he was like half man half creature which was weird.<br /><br />WHAT THE HELL HAVE YOU DONE, SOPHIE ROTH? - 5 stars <br />This short story was just adorable! Sophie hadn't made any friends at her new college that understood her and her sense of humor. By making a comment about Ned Flanders her and Russell form a friendship which turn into more and it's so cute seeing that journey even though it is a short story. I think it's so important that you find someone that is the same weird as you and Sophie did.<br /><br />BEER BUCKETS AND BABY JESUS - 5 stars<br />This one was pretty good. It had me wanting to read and read until it was finished. Vaughn Hatcher was a prankster and also reminds me of a guy i used to like with the same last name. When all people saw was bad in him the pastor at the local church didnt see it in him and neither did his daughtee Gracie. In this short story you see the change in Vaughn, him wanting to be a better person. 'You took it exactly far enough' was a great last sentance.<br /><br />WELCOME TO CHRISTMAS, CA - 5 stars<br />Loved this short story. Ben was the new cook at the dinner and could tell what people actually wanted even if they didnt order it and it brought happiness to them. The owners daughter Maria didnt like it at first. There friendship blossomed and it ended up that Maria looked forward to work. Maria got the best christmas present and the relationship between her and her mother and Rick her restored. On christmas eve Maria went to the<br />effort of creating something special for her and Ben. It was so sweet definitely loved this one. It was adorable <br /><br />STAR OF BETHLEHEM - 5 stars<br />This one would go in my favourites shelf and would have to be my favourite in the book. I didnt want to stop reading. Liddy swapped plans and pretended to be someome else. She fell in love with Ethan and his family and felt it was home. She was so secretive about who she was and you find out why. Love love loved this one.<br /><br />THE GIRL WHO WOKE THE DREAMER - 1 star<br />I started reading this and found i was only reading the words and not getting the story.... the bits of the story i did get were very weird and kind of like a cult. I ended up skimming through the rest of the short story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10150016242773662408" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('M2ofh1nG77U7Y/1ZLgqruxImy00pFz+G1488QqGo8IjvRCfFzgYqTZZsOI1v/JJOcfV07N7pdjo6hpsyhYj6AQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UDw9q2cifnIzoOSeULse2/m0zsQopqbfmZTDJo3a9TuMEgXp8OK7ip6vIUoRTScummdxZd9Y72N0nWRWqfr/sg==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer10555237098201835733">Hi, there! I'm Steph, and I wrote <i>Anna and the French Kiss</i>, <i>Lola and the Boy Next Door</i>, and <i>Isla and the Happily Ever After</i>. I also edited (and contributed a short story to) a romantic holiday anthology called <i>My True Love Gave to Me</i> and its companion anthology, <i>Summer Days and Summer Nights</i>. My next YA release is a horror novel called <i>There's Someone Inside Your House</i>, which will be released Fall</span>
  <span id="freeText10555237098201835733" style="display:none">Hi, there! I'm Steph, and I wrote <i>Anna and the French Kiss</i>, <i>Lola and the Boy Next Door</i>, and <i>Isla and the Happily Ever After</i>. I also edited (and contributed a short story to) a romantic holiday anthology called <i>My True Love Gave to Me</i> and its companion anthology, <i>Summer Days and Summer Nights</i>. My next YA release is a horror novel called <i>There's Someone Inside Your House</i>, which will be released Fall 2017.<br /><br />I don't read blog comments on Goodreads, so if you want to make sure that I receive your message, please click over to my actual blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://stephanieperkins.com/blog/">http://stephanieperkins.com/blog/</a><br /><br />I also don't check my Goodreads inbox. Better ways to reach me are listed here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://stephanieperkins.com/about/">http://stephanieperkins.com/about/</a><br /><br />Instagram: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.instagram.com/naturallystephperkins/">http://www.instagram.com/naturallyste...</a><br />Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://twitter.com/naturallysteph">http://twitter.com/naturallysteph</a><br />8tracks: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://8tracks.com/naturallysteph">http://8tracks.com/naturallysteph</a></span>
